  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {
    background: none;
  }
  a, chops-button, a.button, .button, .linkify {
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: filter 0.3s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.3s ease-in-out;
  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {
    filter: brightness(95%);
  }
  chops-button, a.button, .button {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
    background: var(--chops-white);
    border-radius: 6px;

    margin: 0;
    margin-left: auto;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    padding: var(--chops-button-padding);
  }
  chops-button i.material-icons, a.button i.material-icons, .button i.material-icons {
    display: block;
    margin-right: 4px;
  }
  chops-button.emphasized, a.button.emphasized, .button.emphasized {
    background: var(--chops-primary-button-bg);
    color: var(--chops-primary-button-color);
    text-shadow: 1px 1px 3px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.25);
  }
  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.
  */
  .medium-heading {
    font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);
    font-weight: normal;

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





The vulnerability occurs when the |delegate_|[1] is still holding pointer and it's get deleted then the |delegate_| is being recalled/reused again --> Heap UaF. The code haven't been maintained for a while and it's worth to take a look. 



<span class="line"><!---->The vulnerability occurs when the |delegate_|[1] is still holding pointer and it's get deleted then the |delegate_| is being recalled/reused again --&gt; Heap UaF. The code haven't been maintained for a while and it's worth to take a look. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Also please take a look for PhoneHubTray(), maybe it is effected. The owner  of this functions addressed to 



<span class="line"><!---->Also please take a look for PhoneHubTray(), maybe it is effected. The owner  of this functions addressed to <!----></span>





amehfooz@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/amehfooz@chromium.org"><!---->amehfooz@chromium.org<!----></a>



<br>



<br>

REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





In order to repro this issue, I have tested several ways with different difficulty to repro. The easiest way is using Lacros + tablet mode.



<span class="line"><!---->In order to repro this issue, I have tested several ways with different difficulty to repro. The easiest way is using Lacros + tablet mode.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->Option 1:<!----></span>



<br>





Repro difficulty : hard

<br>





(1) Launch chrome browser. 



<span class="line"><!---->(1) Launch chrome browser. <!----></span>



<br>





(2) Navigate to any YouTube videos and play it.



<span class="line"><!---->(2) Navigate to any YouTube videos and play it.<!----></span>



<br>





(3) After media system tray launch, click PIP repeatedly. 



<span class="line"><!---->(3) After media system tray launch, click PIP repeatedly. <!----></span>



<br>





(4) Sign-out current chrome account to login page with CTRL + SHIFT + Q (2 times).



<span class="line"><!---->(4) Sign-out current chrome account to login page with CTRL + SHIFT + Q (2 times).<!----></span>

(3) Click me then select display 2.



<span class="line"><!---->(3) Click me then select display 2.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->  <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/d621c746479a53e1f7eb1107abd4b600d6de9d69



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/d621c746479a53e1f7eb1107abd4b600d6de9d69"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/d621c746479a53e1f7eb1107abd4b600d6de9d69<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





d621c746479a53e1f7eb1107abd4b600d6de9d69



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/d621c746479a53e1f7eb1107abd4b600d6de9d69"><!---->d621c746479a53e1f7eb1107abd4b600d6de9d69<!----></a>



<br>





Author: Ahmed Mehfooz <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Ahmed Mehfooz &lt;<!----></span>





amehfooz@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/amehfooz@chromium.org"><!---->amehfooz@chromium.org<!----></a>





>



<span class="line"><!---->&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





Date: Fri Jul 08 19:21:57 2022



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Fri Jul 08 19:21:57 2022<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Use WeakPtr for TrayBubbleView::Delegate



<span class="line"><!---->Use WeakPtr for TrayBubbleView::Delegate<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





A race condition during shutdown can result in



<span class="line"><!---->A race condition during shutdown can result in<!----></span>



<br>





the delegate_ ptr in tray_bubble_view to dangle



<span class="line"><!---->the delegate_ ptr in tray_bubble_view to dangle<!----></span>



<br>





resulting in a use-after-free.



<span class="line"><!---->resulting in a use-after-free.<!----></span>



<br>





The bubble is closed via Close(), which is asynchronous, so the widget's destructor doesn't run before shutdown proceeds, leading to the  delegate_  pointer in TrayBubbleView to dangle and use-after-free.



<span class="line"><!---->The bubble is closed via Close(), which is asynchronous, so the widget's destructor doesn't run before shutdown proceeds, leading to the  delegate_  pointer in TrayBubbleView to dangle and use-after-free.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Replacing the raw ptr with a weakPtr to fix the



<span class="line"><!---->Replacing the raw ptr with a weakPtr to fix the<!----></span>



<br>





use-after-free.



<span class="line"><!---->use-after-free.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1336145" title="Security: heap-use-after-free ash/system/tray/tray_bubble_view.cc (chromeOS)"><!---->Bug: 1336145<!----></a>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
